I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Optimizer confluence produces assertion failure in OptStackOps / Opt_a_tossub
**Compiler and OS**
Current cc65 head with MSYS / MINGW64_NT-10.0-19045 3.6.6-2369286a.x86_64 (but I do not believe OS or build system matters).

**Describe the bug**
Certain expressions involving arithmetic with a compare operator (>=) trigger an invariant `CHECK()` in `Opt_a_tossub()` when code is optimized. Please see minimal failing test below. First discovered in the [bug2395.c expansion](https://github.com/avolkov76/cc65/blob/anv-bug-2461/test/val/bug2395.c).

**To Reproduce**
The minimal failing test is:
```C
/* bug #2946: Incomplete, non-removable Rhs asserts in OptStackOps */

#include <stdio.h>
#include <stdlib.h>

unsigned char a, b = 0;
unsigned char c = 10;
unsigned char d = 1;

int main(void) {
    /* 'if' needed to produce a label below, moved by OptJumpTarget3  */
    if (b != 0) {
        /* Operation not important; it only affects the removal of one LDX #$00 */
        b = 0;
    }

    /* d >= 0 is const, A/X=1 (Warning: Result of comparison is always true) */
    a = c - (d >= 0);

    return !(a == 9);
}
```

  1390	
  1391	        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_LDX, AM65_IMM, MakeHexArg (0), 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
  1392	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
  1393	
  1394	        /* Add sign extension - N is unused now */
  1395	        N = CS_GetEntry (D->Code, D->IP);
  1396	        CHECK (N != 0);
  1397	        L = CS_GenLabel (D->Code, N);
  1398	
  1399	        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_BCS, AM65_BRA, L->Name, L, D->OpEntry->LI);
  1400	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
  1401	
  1402	        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_DEX, AM65_IMP, 0, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
  1403	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
  1404	    }
  1405	
  1406	    /* Rhs load entries must be removed */
  1407	    D->Rhs.X.Flags |= LI_REMOVE;
  1408	    D->Rhs.A.Flags |= LI_REMOVE;
  1409	
  1410	    /* Remove the push and the call to the tossubax function */
  1411	    RemoveRemainders (D);
  1412	
  1413	    /* We changed the sequence */
  1414	    return 1;
  1415	}
  1416	
  1417	
  1418	
  1419	static unsigned Opt_a_tosuge (StackOpData* D)
  1420	/* Optimize the tosgeax and tosugeax sequences */
  1421	{
  1422	    return Opt_a_toscmpbool (D, "booluge");
  1423	}
  1424	
  1425	
  1426	
  1427	static unsigned Opt_a_tosugt (StackOpData* D)
  1428	/* Optimize the tosgtax and tosugtax sequences */
  1429	{
  1430	    return Opt_a_toscmpbool (D, "boolugt");
  1431	}

    98	/* Check if Rhs Reg A == Lhs Reg A */
    99	{
   100	    RegInfo* LRI = GetLastChangedRegInfo (D, &D->Lhs.A);
   101	    RegInfo* RRI = GetLastChangedRegInfo (D, &D->Rhs.A);
   102	
   103	    /* RHS can have a -1 ChgIndex only if it is carried over from LHS */
   104	    if (RRI == 0                                    ||
   105	        (D->Rhs.A.ChgIndex >= 0         &&
   106	         D->Rhs.A.ChgIndex == D->Lhs.A.ChgIndex)    ||
   107	        (LRI != 0                       &&
   108	         RegValIsKnown (LRI->Out.RegA)  &&
   109	         RegValIsKnown (RRI->Out.RegA)  &&
   110	         (LRI->Out.RegA & 0xFF) == (RRI->Out.RegA & 0xFF))) {
   111	
   112	        return 1;
   113	    }
   114	
   115	    return 0;
   116

   948	
   949	int IsRegVar (StackOpData* D)
   950	/* If the value pushed is that of a zeropage variable that is unchanged until Op,
   951	** replace ZPLo and ZPHi in the given StackOpData struct by the variable and return true.
   952	** Otherwise leave D untouched and return false.
   953	*/
   954	{
   955	    CodeEntry*  LoadA = D->Lhs.A.LoadEntry;
   956	    CodeEntry*  LoadX = D->Lhs.X.LoadEntry;
   957	    unsigned    Len;
   958	
   959	    /* Must be unchanged till Op */
   960	    if ((D->Lhs.A.Flags & (LI_DIRECT | LI_RELOAD_Y)) != LI_DIRECT ||
   961	        (D->Lhs.X.Flags & (LI_DIRECT | LI_RELOAD_Y)) != LI_DIRECT) {
   962	        return 0;
   963	    }
   964	
   965	    /* Must have both load insns */
   966	    if (LoadA == 0 || LoadX == 0) {
   967	        return 0;
   968	    }
   969	
   970	    /* Must be loads from zp */
   971	    if (LoadA->AM != AM65_ZP || LoadX->AM != AM65_ZP) {
   972	        return 0;
   973	    }
   974	
   975	    /* Must be the same zp loc with high byte in X */
   976	    Len = strlen (LoadA->Arg);
   977	    if (strncmp (LoadA->Arg, LoadX->Arg, Len) != 0      ||
   978	        strcmp (LoadX->Arg + Len, "+1") != 0) {
   979	        return 0;
   980	    }
   981	
   982	    /* Use the zero page location directly */
   983	    D->ZPLo = LoadA->Arg;
   984	    D->ZPHi = LoadX->Arg;
   985	    return 1;
   986	}
   987

   990	void AddStoreLhsA (StackOpData* D)
   991	/* Add a store to zero page after the push insn */
   992	{
   993	    CodeEntry* X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_STA, AM65_ZP, D->ZPLo, 0, D->PushEntry->LI);
   994	    InsertEntry (D, X, D->PushIndex+1);
   995	}

   999	void AddStoreLhsX (StackOpData* D)
  1000	/* Add a store to zero page after the push insn */
  1001	{
  1002	    CodeEntry* X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_STX, AM65_ZP, D->ZPHi, 0, D->PushEntry->LI);
  1003	    InsertEntry (D, X, D->PushIndex+1);
  1004	}

  1007	
  1008	void ReplacePushByStore (StackOpData* D)
  1009	/* Replace the call to the push subroutine by a store into the zero page
  1010	** location (actually, the push is not replaced, because we need it for
  1011	** later, but the name is still ok since the push will get removed at the
  1012	** end of each routine).
  1013	*/
  1014	{
  1015	    /* Store the value into the zeropage instead of pushing it. Check high
  1016	    ** byte first so that the store is later in A/X order.
  1017	    */
  1018	    if ((D->Lhs.X.Flags & LI_DIRECT) == 0) {
  1019	        AddStoreLhsX (D);
  1020	    }
  1021	    if ((D->Lhs.A.Flags & LI_DIRECT) == 0) {
  1022	        AddStoreLhsA (D);
  1023	    }
  1024	}

  1029	/* Add an op for the low byte of an operator. This function honours the
  1030	** OP_DIRECT and OP_RELOAD_Y flags and generates the necessary instructions.
  1031	** All code is inserted at the current insertion point.
  1032	*/
  1033	{
  1034	    CodeEntry* X;
  1035	
  1036	    if ((LI->A.Flags & LI_DIRECT) != 0) {
  1037	        /* Op with a variable location. If the location is on the stack, we
  1038	        ** need to reload the Y register.
  1039	        */
  1040	        if ((LI->A.Flags & LI_RELOAD_Y) == 0) {
  1041	
  1042	            /* opc ... */
  1043	            CodeEntry* LoadA = LI->A.LoadEntry;
  1044	            X = NewCodeEntry (OPC, LoadA->AM, LoadA->Arg, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
  1045	            InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
  1046	
  1047	        } else {
  1048	
  1049	            if ((LI->A.Flags & LI_CHECK_Y) == 0) {
  1050	                /* ldy #offs */
  1051	                X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_LDY, AM65_IMM, MakeHexArg (LI->A.Offs), 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
  1052	            } else {
  1053	                /* ldy src */
  1054	                X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_LDY, LI->A.LoadYEntry->AM, LI->A.LoadYEntry->Arg, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
  1055	            }
  1056	            InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
  1057

  1059	                /* opc (c_sp),y */

  1064	            }

  1207	void RemoveRemainders (StackOpData* D)
  1208	/* Remove the code that is unnecessary after translation of the sequence */
  1209	{
  1210	    /* Remove the register loads for lhs and rhs if nothing prevents that */
  1211	    RemoveRegLoads (D, &D->Lhs);
  1212	    RemoveRegLoads (D, &D->Rhs);
  1213	
  1214	    /* Remove the push and the operator routine */
  1215	    DelEntry (D, D->OpIndex);
  1216	    DelEntry (D, D->PushIndex);
  1217	}

  1821	    if ((D->ZPUsage & REG_PTR1) == REG_NONE) {

  1841	/*****************************************************************************/
  1842	/*                                   Code                                    */
  1843	/*****************************************************************************/
  1844	
  1845	
  1846	
  1847	unsigned OptStackOps (CodeSeg* S)
  1848	/* Optimize operations that take operands via the stack */
  1849	{
  1850	    unsigned        Changes = 0;        /* Number of changes in one run */
  1851	    StackOpData     Data;
  1852	    int             I;
  1853	    int             OldEntryCount;      /* Old number of entries */
  1854	    unsigned        Used;               /* What registers would be used */
  1855	    unsigned        PushedRegs = 0;     /* Track if the same regs are used after the push */
  1856	    int             RhsAChgIndex;       /* Track if rhs is changed more than once */
  1857	    int             RhsXChgIndex;       /* Track if rhs is changed more than once */
  1858	    int             IsRegAOptFunc = 0;  /* Whether to use the RegA-only optimizations */
  1859	
  1860	    enum {
  1861	        Initialize,
  1862	        Search,
  1863	        FoundPush,
  1864	        FoundOp
  1865	    } State = Initialize;
  1866	
  1867	
  1868	    /* Remember the code segment in the info struct */
  1869	    Data.Code = S;
  1870	
  1871	    /* Look for a call to pushax followed by a call to some other function
  1872	    ** that takes it's first argument on the stack, and the second argument
  1873	    ** in the primary register.
  1874	    ** It depends on the code between the two if we can handle/transform the
  1875	    ** sequence, so check this code for the following list of things:
  1876	    **
  1877	    **  - the range must be a basic block (one entry, one exit)
  1878	    **  - there may not be accesses to local variables with unknown
  1879	    **    offsets (because we have to adjust these offsets).
  1880	    **  - no subroutine calls
  1881	    **  - no jump labels
  1882	    **
  1883	    ** Since we need a zero page register later, do also check the
  1884	    ** intermediate code for zero page use.
  1885	    ** When hibytes of both oprands are equal, we may have more specialized
  1886	    ** optimization for the op.
  1887	    */
  1888	    I = 0;
  1889	    while (I < (int)CS_GetEntryCount (S)) {
  1890	
  1891	        /* Get the next entry */
  1892	        CodeEntry* E = CS_GetEntry (S, I);
  1893	
  1894	        /* Actions depend on state */
  1895	        switch (State) {
  1896	
  1897	            case Initialize:
  1898	                ResetStackOpData (&Data);
  1899	                State = Search;
  1900	                /* FALLTHROUGH */
  1901	
  1902	            case Search:
  1903	                /* While searching, track register load insns, so we can tell
  1904	                ** what is in a register once pushax is encountered.
  1905	                */
  1906	                if (CE_HasLabel (E)) {
  1907	                    /* Currently we don't track across branches.
  1908	                    ** Treat this as a change to all regs.
  1909	                    */
  1910	                    ClearLoadInfo (&Data.Lhs);
  1911	                    Data.Lhs.A.ChgIndex = I;
  1912	                    Data.Lhs.X.ChgIndex = I;
  1913	                    Data.Lhs.Y.ChgIndex = I;
  1914	                }
  1915	                if (CE_IsCallTo (E, "pushax")) {
  1916	                    /* Disallow removing Lhs loads if the registers are used */
  1917	                    SetIfOperandLoadUnremovable (&Data.Lhs, Data.UsedRegs);
  1918	
  1919	                    /* The Lhs regs are also used as the default Rhs until changed */
  1920	                    PushedRegs = REG_AXY;
  1921	                    CopyLoadInfo (&Data.Rhs, &Data.Lhs);
  1922	
  1923	                    Data.PushIndex = I;
  1924	                    Data.PushEntry = E;
  1925	                    State = FoundPush;
  1926	                } else {
  1927	                    /* Track load insns */
  1928	                    Used = TrackLoads (&Data.Lhs, S, I);
  1929	                    Data.UsedRegs &= ~E->Chg;
  1930	                    Data.UsedRegs |= Used;
  1931	                }
  1932	                break;
  1933	
  1934	            case FoundPush:
  1935	                /* We' found a pushax before. Search for a stack op that may
  1936	                ** follow and in the meantime, track zeropage usage and check
  1937	                ** for code that will disable us from translating the sequence.
  1938	                */
  1939	                if (CE_HasLabel (E)) {
  1940	                    /* Currently we don't track across branches.
  1941	                    ** Treat this as a change to all regs.
  1942	                    */
  1943	                    ClearLoadInfo (&Data.Rhs);
  1944	                    Data.Rhs.A.ChgIndex = I;
  1945	                    Data.Rhs.X.ChgIndex = I;
  1946	                    Data.Rhs.Y.ChgIndex = I;
  1947	                }
  1948	                if (E->OPC == OP65_JSR) {
  1949	                    /* Subroutine call: Check if this is one of the functions,
  1950	                    ** we're going to replace.
  1951	                    */
  1952	                    if (SameRegXValue (&Data)) {
  1953	                        Data.OptFunc = FindFunc (FuncRegATable, FUNC_COUNT (FuncRegATable), E->Arg);
  1954	                        IsRegAOptFunc = 1;
  1955	                    }
  1956	                    if (Data.OptFunc == 0) {
  1957	                        Data.OptFunc = FindFunc (FuncTable, FUNC_COUNT (FuncTable), E->Arg);
  1958	                        IsRegAOptFunc = 0;
  1959	                    }
  1960	                    if (Data.OptFunc) {
  1961	                        /* Disallow removing Rhs loads if the registers are used */
  1962	                        SetIfOperandLoadUnremovable (&Data.Rhs, Data.UsedRegs);
  1963	
  1964	                        /* Remember the op index and go on */
  1965	                        Data.OpIndex = I;
  1966	                        Data.OpEntry = E;
  1967	                        State = FoundOp;
  1968	                        break;
  1969	                    } else if (!HarmlessCall (E, 2)) {
  1970	                        /* The call might use or change the content that we are
  1971	                        ** going to access later via the stack pointer. In any
  1972	                        ** case, we need to start over after the last pushax.
  1973	                        ** Note: This will also happen if we encounter a call
  1974	                        ** to pushax!
  1975	                        */
  1976	                        I = Data.PushIndex;
  1977	                        State = Initialize;
  1978	                        break;
  1979	                    }
  1980	                } else if (((E->Chg | E->Use) & REG_SP) != 0) {
  1981	
  1982	                    /* If we are using the stack, and we don't have "indirect Y"
  1983	                    ** addressing mode, or the value of Y is unknown, or less
  1984	                    ** than two, we cannot cope with this piece of code. Having
  1985	                    ** an unknown value of Y means that we cannot correct the
  1986	                    ** stack offset, while having an offset less than two means
  1987	                    ** that the code works with the value on stack which is to
  1988	                    ** be removed.
  1989	                    */
  1990	                    if (E->AM == AM65_ZPX_IND               ||
  1991	                        ((E->Chg | E->Use) & SLV_IND) == 0  ||
  1992	                        (RegValIsUnknown (E->RI->In.RegY)   ||
  1993	                         E->RI->In.RegY < 2)) {
  1994	                        I = Data.PushIndex;
  1995	                        State = Initialize;
  1996	                        break;
  1997	                    }
  1998	
  1999	                }
  2000	
  2001	                /* Memorize the old rhs load indices before refreshing them */
  2002	                RhsAChgIndex = Data.Rhs.A.ChgIndex;
  2003	                RhsXChgIndex = Data.Rhs.X.ChgIndex;
  2004	
  2005	                /* Keep tracking Lhs src if necessary */
  2006	                SetIfOperandSrcAffected (&Data.Lhs, E);
  2007	
  2008	                /* Track register usage */
  2009	                Used = TrackLoads (&Data.Rhs, S, I);
  2010	
  2011	                Data.ZPUsage   |= (E->Use | E->Chg);
  2012	                /* The changes could depend on the use */
  2013	                Data.UsedRegs  &= ~E->Chg;
  2014	                Data.UsedRegs  |= Used;
  2015	                Data.ZPChanged |= E->Chg;
  2016	
  2017	                /* Check if any parts of Lhs are used again before overwritten */
  2018	                if (PushedRegs != 0) {
  2019	                    if ((PushedRegs & E->Use) != 0) {
  2020	                        SetIfOperandLoadUnremovable (&Data.Lhs, PushedRegs & E->Use);
  2021	                    }
  2022	                    PushedRegs &= ~E->Chg;
  2023	                }
  2024	                /* Check if rhs is changed again after the push */
  2025	                if ((RhsAChgIndex != Data.Lhs.A.ChgIndex &&
  2026	                     RhsAChgIndex != Data.Rhs.A.ChgIndex)       ||
  2027	                    (RhsXChgIndex != Data.Lhs.X.ChgIndex &&
  2028	                     RhsXChgIndex != Data.Rhs.X.ChgIndex)) {
  2029	                    /* This will disable those sub-opts that require removing
  2030	                    ** the rhs as they can't handle such cases correctly.
  2031	                    */
  2032	                    Data.RhsMultiChg = 1;
  2033	                }
  2034	                break;
  2035	
  2036	            case FoundOp:
  2037	                /* Track zero page location usage beyond this point */
  2038	                Data.ZPUsage |= GetRegInfo (S, I, REG_SREG | REG_PTR1 | REG_PTR2);
  2039	
  2040	                /* Finalize the load info */
  2041	                FinalizeLoadInfo (&Data.Lhs, S);
  2042	                FinalizeLoadInfo (&Data.Rhs, S);
  2043	
  2044	                /* Check if the lhs loads from zeropage. If this is true, these
  2045	                ** zero page locations have to be added to ZPUsage, because
  2046	                ** they cannot be used for intermediate storage. In addition,
  2047	                ** if one of these zero page locations is destroyed between
  2048	                ** pushing the lhs and the actual operation, we cannot use the
  2049	                ** original zero page locations for the final op, but must
  2050	                ** use another ZP location to save them.
  2051	                */
  2052	                Data.ZPChanged &= REG_ZP;
  2053	                if (Data.Lhs.A.LoadEntry && Data.Lhs.A.LoadEntry->AM == AM65_ZP) {
  2054	                    Data.ZPUsage |= Data.Lhs.A.LoadEntry->Use;
  2055	                    if ((Data.Lhs.A.LoadEntry->Use & Data.ZPChanged) != 0) {
  2056	                        Data.Lhs.A.Flags &= ~(LI_DIRECT | LI_RELOAD_Y);
  2057	                    }
  2058	                }
  2059	                if (Data.Lhs.X.LoadEntry && Data.Lhs.X.LoadEntry->AM == AM65_ZP) {
  2060	                    Data.ZPUsage |= Data.Lhs.X.LoadEntry->Use;
  2061	                    if ((Data.Lhs.X.LoadEntry->Use & Data.ZPChanged) != 0) {
  2062	                        Data.Lhs.X.Flags &= ~(LI_DIRECT | LI_RELOAD_Y);
  2063	                    }
  2064	                }
  2065	
  2066	                /* Flag entries that can't be removed */
  2067	                SetDontRemoveEntryFlags (&Data);
  2068	
  2069	                /* Check the preconditions. If they aren't ok, reset the insn
  2070	                ** pointer to the pushax and start over. We will lose part of
  2071	                ** load tracking but at least a/x has probably lost between
  2072	                ** pushax and here and will be tracked again when restarting.
  2073	                */
  2074	                if (IsRegAOptFunc ? !RegAPreCondOk (&Data) : !PreCondOk (&Data)) {
  2075	                    /* Unflag entries that can't be removed */
  2076	                    ResetDontRemoveEntryFlags (&Data);
  2077	                    I = Data.PushIndex;
  2078	                    State = Initialize;
  2079	                    break;
  2080	                }
  2081	
  2082	                /* Prepare the remainder of the data structure. */
  2083	                Data.PrevEntry = CS_GetPrevEntry (S, Data.PushIndex);
  2084	                Data.PushEntry = CS_GetEntry (S, Data.PushIndex);
  2085	                Data.OpEntry   = CS_GetEntry (S, Data.OpIndex);
  2086	                Data.NextEntry = CS_GetNextEntry (S, Data.OpIndex);
  2087	
  2088	                /* Remember the current number of code lines */
  2089	                OldEntryCount = CS_GetEntryCount (S);
  2090	
  2091	                /* Adjust stack offsets to account for the upcoming removal */
  2092	                AdjustStackOffset (&Data, 2);
  2093	
  2094	                /* Regenerate register info, since AdjustStackOffset changed
  2095	                ** the code
  2096	                */
  2097	                CS_GenRegInfo (S);
  2098	
  2099	                /* Call the optimizer function */
  2100	                const OptFuncDesc* Desc = Data.OptFunc;
  2101	                Changes += Desc->Func (&Data);
  2102	
  2103	                /* Unflag entries that can't be removed */
  2104	                ResetDontRemoveEntryFlags (&Data);
  2105

   121	static int SameRegXValue (StackOpData* D)
   122	/* Check if Rhs Reg X == Lhs Reg X */
   123	{
   124	    RegInfo* LRI = GetLastChangedRegInfo (D, &D->Lhs.X);
   125	    RegInfo* RRI = GetLastChangedRegInfo (D, &D->Rhs.X);
   126	
   127	    if (RRI == 0                                    ||
   128	        (D->Rhs.X.ChgIndex >= 0         &&
   129	         D->Rhs.X.ChgIndex == D->Lhs.X.ChgIndex)    ||
   130	        (LRI != 0                       &&
   131	         RegValIsKnown (LRI->Out.RegX)  &&
   132	         RegValIsKnown (RRI->Out.RegX)  &&
   133	         (LRI->Out.RegX & 0xFF) == (RRI->Out.RegX & 0xFF))) {
   134	
   135	        return 1;
   136	    }
   137	
   138	    return 0;
   139	
   140	}

   150	static unsigned Opt_toseqax_tosneax (StackOpData* D, const char* BoolTransformer)
   151	/* Optimize the toseqax and tosneax sequences. */
   152	{
   153	    CodeEntry*  X;
   154	    CodeLabel* L;
   155	
   156	    /* Create a call to the boolean transformer function and a label for this
   157	    ** insn. This is needed for all variants. Other insns are inserted *before*
   158	    ** the call.
   159	    */
   160	    X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_JSR, AM65_ABS, BoolTransformer, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
   161	    InsertEntry (D, X, D->OpIndex + 1);
   162	    L = CS_GenLabel (D->Code, X);
   163	
   164	    /* If the lhs is direct (but not stack relative), encode compares with lhs
   165	    ** effectively reverting the order (which doesn't matter for ==).
   166	    */
   167	    if ((D->Lhs.A.Flags & (LI_DIRECT | LI_RELOAD_Y)) == LI_DIRECT &&
   168	        (D->Lhs.X.Flags & (LI_DIRECT | LI_RELOAD_Y)) == LI_DIRECT) {
   169	
   170	        CodeEntry* LoadX = D->Lhs.X.LoadEntry;
   171	        CodeEntry* LoadA = D->Lhs.A.LoadEntry;
   172	
   173	        D->IP = D->OpIndex+1;
   174	
   175	        /* cpx */
   176	        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_CPX, LoadX->AM, LoadX->Arg, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
   177	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   178	
   179	        /* bne L */
   180	        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_BNE, AM65_BRA, L->Name, L, D->OpEntry->LI);
   181	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   182	
   183	        /* cmp */
   184	        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_CMP, LoadA->AM, LoadA->Arg, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
   185	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   186	
   187	        /* Lhs load entries can be removed if not used later */
   188	        D->Lhs.X.Flags |= LI_REMOVE;
   189	        D->Lhs.A.Flags |= LI_REMOVE;
   190	
   191	    } else if ((D->Rhs.A.Flags & (LI_DIRECT | LI_RELOAD_Y)) == LI_DIRECT &&
   192	               (D->Rhs.X.Flags & (LI_DIRECT | LI_RELOAD_Y)) == LI_DIRECT &&
   193	               D->RhsMultiChg == 0) {
   194	
   195	        CodeEntry* LoadX = D->Rhs.X.LoadEntry;
   196	        CodeEntry* LoadA = D->Rhs.A.LoadEntry;
   197	
   198	        D->IP = D->OpIndex+1;
   199	
   200	        /* cpx */
   201	        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_CPX, LoadX->AM, LoadX->Arg, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
   202	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   203	
   204	        /* bne L */
   205	        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_BNE, AM65_BRA, L->Name, L, D->OpEntry->LI);
   206	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   207	
   208	        /* cmp */
   209	        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_CMP, LoadA->AM, LoadA->Arg, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
   210	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   211	
   212	        /* Rhs load entries must be removed */
   213	        D->Rhs.X.Flags |= LI_REMOVE;
   214	        D->Rhs.A.Flags |= LI_REMOVE;
   215	
   216	    } else if ((D->Rhs.A.Flags & LI_DIRECT) != 0 &&
   217	               (D->Rhs.X.Flags & LI_DIRECT) != 0) {
   218	
   219	        D->IP = D->OpIndex+1;
   220	
   221	        /* Add operand for low byte */
   222	        AddOpLow (D, OP65_CMP, &D->Rhs);
   223	
   224	        /* bne L */
   225	        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_BNE, AM65_BRA, L->Name, L, D->OpEntry->LI);
   226	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   227	
   228	        /* Add operand for high byte */
   229	        AddOpHigh (D, OP65_CMP, &D->Rhs, 0);
   230	
   231	    } else {
   232	
   233	        /* Save lhs into zeropage, then compare */
   234	        AddStoreLhsX (D);
   235	        AddStoreLhsA (D);
   236	
   237	        D->IP = D->OpIndex+1;
   238	
   239	        /* cpx */

   241	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);

   244	        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_BNE, AM65_BRA, L->Name, L, D->OpEntry->LI);
   245	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   246	
   247	        /* cmp */
   248	        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_CMP, AM65_ZP, D->ZPLo, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
   249	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   250	
   251	    }
   252	
   253	    /* Remove the push and the call to the tosgeax function */
   254	    RemoveRemainders (D);
   255	
   256	    /* We changed the sequence */
   257	    return 1;
   258	}

   262	static unsigned Opt_tosshift (StackOpData* D, const char* Name)
   263	/* Optimize shift sequences. */
   264	{
   265	    CodeEntry*  X;
   266	
   267	    /* If the lhs is direct (but not stack relative), we can just reload the
   268	    ** data later.
   269	    */
   270	    if ((D->Lhs.A.Flags & (LI_DIRECT | LI_RELOAD_Y)) == LI_DIRECT &&
   271	        (D->Lhs.X.Flags & (LI_DIRECT | LI_RELOAD_Y)) == LI_DIRECT) {
   272	
   273	        CodeEntry* LoadX = D->Lhs.X.LoadEntry;
   274	        CodeEntry* LoadA = D->Lhs.A.LoadEntry;
   275	
   276	        /* Inline the shift */
   277	        D->IP = D->OpIndex+1;
   278	
   279	        /* tay */
   280	        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_TAY, AM65_IMP, 0, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
   281	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   282	
   283	        /* lda */
   284	        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_LDA, LoadA->AM, LoadA->Arg, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
   285	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   286	
   287	        /* ldx */
   288	        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_LDX, LoadX->AM, LoadX->Arg, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
   289	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   290	
   291	        /* Lhs load entries can be removed if not used later */
   292	        D->Lhs.X.Flags |= LI_REMOVE;
   293	        D->Lhs.A.Flags |= LI_REMOVE;
   294	
   295	    } else {
   296	
   297	        /* Save lhs into zeropage and reload later */
   298	        AddStoreLhsX (D);
   299	        AddStoreLhsA (D);
   300	
   301	        /* Be sure to setup IP after adding the stores, otherwise it will get
   302	        ** messed up.
   303	        */
   304	        D->IP = D->OpIndex+1;
   305	
   306	        /* tay */
   307	        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_TAY, AM65_IMP, 0, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
   308	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   309	
   310	        /* lda zp */
   311	        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_LDA, AM65_ZP, D->ZPLo, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
   312	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   313	
   314	        /* ldx zp+1 */
   315	        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_LDX, AM65_ZP, D->ZPHi, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
   316	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   317	
   318	    }
   319	
   320	    /* jsr shlaxy/aslaxy/whatever */
   321	    X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_JSR, AM65_ABS, Name, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
   322	    InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   323	
   324	    /* Remove the push and the call to the shift function */
   325	    RemoveRemainders (D);
   326	
   327	    /* We changed the sequence */
   328	    return 1;
   329	}

   333	static unsigned Opt___bzero (StackOpData* D)
   334	/* Optimize the __bzero sequence */
   335	{
   336	    CodeEntry*  X;
   337	    const char* Arg;
   338	    CodeLabel*  L;

   354	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->OpIndex+2);

   356	
   357	    /* X is always zero, A contains the size of the data area to zero.
   358	    ** Note: A may be zero, in which case the operation is null op.
   359	    */
   360	    if (D->OpEntry->RI->In.RegA != 0) {

    56	    LI_DIRECT       = 0x01,         /* Direct op may be used */
    57	    LI_RELOAD_Y     = 0x02,         /* Reload index register Y */
    58	    LI_REMOVE       = 0x04,         /* Load may be removed */

    67	    LI_Y_CHG        = 0x0800,       /* Opc addressing Y is possibly modified */

    70	    LI_USED_BY_Y    = 0x4000,       /* Content used by RegY */

    72	    LI_LOAD_INSN    = 0x010000,     /* Is a load insn */

   514	static unsigned Opt_tosaddax (StackOpData* D)
   515	/* Optimize the tosaddax sequence */
   516	{
   517	    CodeEntry*  X;
   518	    CodeEntry*  N;
   519	
   520	    /* We need the entry behind the add */
   521	    CHECK (D->NextEntry != 0);
   522	
   523	    /* Check if the X register is known and zero when the add is done, and
   524	    ** if the add is followed by
   525	    **
   526	    **  ldy     #$00
   527	    **  jsr     ldauidx         ; or ldaidx
   528	    **
   529	    ** If this is true, the addition does actually add an offset to a pointer
   530	    ** before it is dereferenced. Since both subroutines take an offset in Y,
   531	    ** we can pass the offset (instead of #$00) and remove the addition
   532	    ** alltogether.
   533	    */
   534	    if (D->OpEntry->RI->In.RegX == 0                            &&
   535	        D->NextEntry->OPC == OP65_LDY                           &&
   536	        CE_IsKnownImm (D->NextEntry, 0)                         &&
   537	        !CE_HasLabel (D->NextEntry)                             &&
   538	        (N = CS_GetNextEntry (D->Code, D->OpIndex + 1)) != 0    &&
   539	        (CE_IsCallTo (N, "ldauidx")                     ||
   540	         CE_IsCallTo (N, "ldaidx"))) {
   541	
   542	        int Signed = (strcmp (N->Arg, "ldaidx") == 0);
   543	
   544	        /* Store the value into the zeropage instead of pushing it */
   545	        AddStoreLhsX (D);
   546	        AddStoreLhsA (D);
   547	
   548	        /* Replace the ldy by a tay. Be sure to create the new entry before
   549	        ** deleting the ldy, since we will reference the line info from this
   550	        ** insn.
   551	        */
   552	        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_TAY, AM65_IMP, 0, 0, D->NextEntry->LI);
   553	        DelEntry (D, D->OpIndex + 1);
   554	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->OpIndex + 1);
   555	
   556	        /* Replace the call to ldaidx/ldauidx. Since X is already zero, and
   557	        ** the ptr is in the zero page location, we just need to load from
   558	        ** the pointer, and fix X in case of ldaidx.
   559	        */
   560	        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_LDA, AM65_ZP_INDY, D->ZPLo, 0, N->LI);
   561	        DelEntry (D, D->OpIndex + 2);
   562	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->OpIndex + 2);
   563	        if (Signed) {
   564	
   565	            CodeLabel* L;
   566	
   567	            /* Add sign extension - N is unused now */
   568	            N = CS_GetNextEntry (D->Code, D->OpIndex + 2);
   569	            CHECK (N != 0);
   570	            L = CS_GenLabel (D->Code, N);
   571	
   572	            X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_BPL, AM65_BRA, L->Name, L, X->LI);
   573	            InsertEntry (D, X, D->OpIndex + 3);
   574	
   575	            X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_DEX, AM65_IMP, 0, 0, X->LI);
   576	            InsertEntry (D, X, D->OpIndex + 4);
   577	        }
   578	
   579	    } else {
   580	
   581	        /* Store the value into the zeropage instead of pushing it */
   582	        ReplacePushByStore (D);
   583	
   584	        /* Inline the add */
   585	        D->IP = D->OpIndex+1;
   586	
   587	        /* clc */
   588	        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_CLC, AM65_IMP, 0, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
   589	        InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   590	
   591	        /* Low byte */
   592	        AddOpLow (D, OP65_ADC, &D->Lhs);
   593	
   594	        /* High byte */
   595	        if (D->PushEntry->RI->In.RegX == 0) {
   596	
   597	            /* The high byte is the value in X plus the carry */
   598	            CodeLabel* L = CS_GenLabel (D->Code, D->NextEntry);
   599	
   600	            /* bcc L */
   601	            X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_BCC, AM65_BRA, L->Name, L, D->OpEntry->LI);
   602	            InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   603	
   604	            /* inx */
   605	            X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_INX, AM65_IMP, 0, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
   606	            InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   607	
   608	        } else if (D->OpEntry->RI->In.RegX == 0                         &&
   609	                   (RegValIsKnown (D->PushEntry->RI->In.RegX)   ||
   610	                    (D->Lhs.X.Flags & LI_RELOAD_Y) == 0)) {
   611	
   612	            /* The high byte is that of the first operand plus carry */
   613	            CodeLabel* L;
   614	            if (RegValIsKnown (D->PushEntry->RI->In.RegX)) {
   615	                /* Value of first op high byte is known */
   616	                const char* Arg = MakeHexArg (D->PushEntry->RI->In.RegX);
   617	                X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_LDX, AM65_IMM, Arg, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
   618	            } else {
   619	                /* Value of first op high byte is unknown. Load from ZP or
   620	                ** original storage.
   621	                */
   622	                if (D->Lhs.X.Flags & LI_DIRECT) {
   623	                    CodeEntry* LoadX = D->Lhs.X.LoadEntry;
   624	                    X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_LDX, LoadX->AM, LoadX->Arg, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
   625	                } else {
   626	                    X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_LDX, AM65_ZP, D->ZPHi, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
   627	                }
   628	            }
   629	            InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   630	
   631	            /* bcc label */
   632	            L = CS_GenLabel (D->Code, D->NextEntry);
   633	            X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_BCC, AM65_BRA, L->Name, L, D->OpEntry->LI);
   634	            InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   635	
   636	            /* inx */
   637	            X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_INX, AM65_IMP, 0, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
   638	            InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   639	        } else {
   640	            /* High byte is unknown */
   641	            AddOpHigh (D, OP65_ADC, &D->Lhs, 1);
   642	        }
   643	    }
   644	
   645	    /* Remove the push and the call to the tosaddax function */
   646	    RemoveRemainders (D);
   647	
   648	    /* We changed the sequence */
   649	    return 1;
   650	}

   654	static unsigned Opt_tosandax (StackOpData* D)
   655	/* Optimize the tosandax sequence */
   656	{
   657	    /* Store the value into the zeropage instead of pushing it */
   658	    ReplacePushByStore (D);
   659	
   660	    /* Inline the and, low byte */
   661	    D->IP = D->OpIndex + 1;
   662	    AddOpLow (D, OP65_AND, &D->Lhs);
   663	
   664	    /* High byte */
   665	    AddOpHigh (D, OP65_AND, &D->Lhs, 1);
   666	
   667	    /* Remove the push and the call to the tosandax function */
   668	    RemoveRemainders (D);
   669	
   670	    /* We changed the sequence */
   671	    return 1;
   672	}

   860	
   861	static unsigned Opt_tossubax (StackOpData* D)
   862	/* Optimize the tossubax sequence. Note: subtraction is not commutative! */
   863	{
   864	    CodeEntry*  X;
   865	
   866	
   867	    /* Inline the sbc */
   868	    D->IP = D->OpIndex+1;
   869	
   870	    /* sec */
   871	    X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_SEC, AM65_IMP, 0, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
   872	    InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
   873	
   874	    /* Must be true because of OP_RHS_LOAD */
   875	    CHECK ((D->Rhs.A.Flags & D->Rhs.X.Flags & LI_DIRECT) != 0);
   876	
   877	    /* Add code for low operand */
   878	    AddOpLow (D, OP65_SBC, &D->Rhs);
   879	
   880	    /* Add code for high operand */
   881	    AddOpHigh (D, OP65_SBC, &D->Rhs, 1);
   882	
   883	    /* Rhs load entries must be removed */
   884	    D->Rhs.X.Flags |= LI_REMOVE;
   885	    D->Rhs.A.Flags |= LI_REMOVE;
   886	
   887	    /* Remove the push and the call to the tossubax function */
   888	    RemoveRemainders (D);
   889

   900

   904	
   905	    /* Must be true because of OP_RHS_LOAD */

   924	    InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);

   495	void SetIfOperandLoadUnremovable (LoadInfo* LI, unsigned Used)
   496	/* Check and flag operand load that may be unremovable */
   497	{
   498	    /* Disallow removing the loads if the registers are used */
   499	    if ((Used & REG_A) != 0) {
   500	        LI->A.Flags |= LI_DONT_REMOVE;
   501	    }
   502	    if ((Used & REG_X) != 0) {
   503	        LI->X.Flags |= LI_DONT_REMOVE;
   504	    }
   505	    if ((Used & REG_Y) != 0) {
   506	        LI->Y.Flags |= LI_DONT_REMOVE;
   507	    }
   508	}

   511	
   512	unsigned int TrackLoads (LoadInfo* LI, CodeSeg* S, int I)
   513	/* Track loads for a code entry.
   514	** Return used registers.
   515	*/
   516	{
   517	    unsigned Used;
   518	    CodeEntry* E = CS_GetEntry (S, I);
   519	    CHECK (E != 0);
   520	
   521	    /* By default */
   522	    Used = E->Use;
   523	
   524	    /* Whether we had a load or xfer op before or not, the newly loaded value
   525	    ** will be the real one used for the pushax/op unless it's overwritten,
   526	    ** so we can just reset the flags about it in such cases.
   527	    */
   528	    if (E->Info & OF_LOAD) {
   529	
   530	        LoadRegInfo* LRI = 0;
   531	
   532	        /* Determine, which register was loaded */
   533	        if (E->Chg & REG_A) {
   534	            LRI = &LI->A;
   535	        } else if (E->Chg & REG_X) {
   536	            LRI = &LI->X;
   537	        } else if (E->Chg & REG_Y) {
   538	            LRI = &LI->Y;
   539	        }
   540	        CHECK (LRI != 0);
   541	
   542	        /* Remember the load */
   543	        LRI->LoadIndex  = I;
   544	        LRI->ChgIndex   = I;
   545	        LRI->LoadYIndex = -1;
   546	
   547	        /* Set load flags */
   548	        LRI->Flags = LI_LOAD_INSN;
   549	        if (E->AM == AM65_IMM) {
   550	            /* These insns are all ok and replaceable */
   551	            LRI->Flags |= LI_DIRECT;
   552	        } else if (E->AM == AM65_ZP || E->AM == AM65_ABS) {
   553	            /* These insns are replaceable only if they are not modified later */
   554	            LRI->Flags |= LI_CHECK_ARG;
   555	        } else if (E->AM == AM65_ZPY || E->AM == AM65_ABSY) {
   556	            /* These insns are replaceable only if they are not modified later */
   557	            LRI->Flags |= LI_CHECK_ARG | LI_CHECK_Y;
   558	        } else if (E->AM == AM65_ZP_INDY &&
   559	                   strcmp (E->Arg, "c_sp") == 0) {
   560	            /* A load from the stack with known offset is also ok, but in this
   561	            ** case we must reload the index register later. Please note that
   562	            ** a load indirect via other zero page locations is not ok, since
   563	            ** these locations may change between the push and the actual
   564	            ** operation.
   565	            */
   566	            LRI->Flags |= LI_CHECK_ARG | LI_CHECK_Y | LI_SP;
   567	
   568	            /* Reg Y can be regarded as unused if this load is removed */
   569	            Used &= ~REG_Y;
   570	            if (LRI == &LI->A) {
   571	                LI->Y.Flags |= LI_USED_BY_A;
   572	            } else {
   573	                LI->Y.Flags |= LI_USED_BY_X;
   574	            }
   575	        }
   576	
   577	        /* If the load offset has a known value, we can just remember and reload
   578	        ** it into the index register later.
   579	        */
   580	        if ((LRI->Flags & LI_CHECK_Y) != 0) {
   581	            if (RegValIsKnown (E->RI->In.RegY)) {
   582	                LRI->Offs = (unsigned char)E->RI->In.RegY;
   583	                LRI->Flags &= ~LI_CHECK_Y;
   584	                LRI->Flags |= LI_RELOAD_Y;
   585	            } else {
   586	                /* We need to check if the src of Y is changed */
   587	                LRI->LoadYIndex = LI->Y.LoadIndex;
   588	            }
   589	        }
   590	
   591	        /* Watch for any change of the load target */
   592	        if ((LRI->Flags & LI_CHECK_ARG) != 0) {
   593	            LRI->LoadEntry = CS_GetEntry (S, I);
   594	        }
   595	
   596	        if (LRI->LoadYIndex >= 0) {
   597	            LRI->LoadYEntry = CS_GetEntry (S, LRI->LoadYIndex);
   598	        } else {
   599	            LRI->LoadYEntry = 0;
   600	        }
   601	
   602	    } else if (E->Info & OF_XFR) {
   603	
   604	        /* Determine source and target of the transfer and handle the TSX insn */
   605	        LoadRegInfo* Src;
   606	        LoadRegInfo* Tgt;
   607	        switch (E->OPC) {
   608	            case OP65_TAX:
   609	                Src = &LI->A;
   610	                Tgt = &LI->X;
   611	                Used &= ~REG_A;
   612	                Src->Flags |= LI_USED_BY_X;
   613	                break;
   614	            case OP65_TAY:
   615	                Src = &LI->A;
   616	                Tgt = &LI->Y;
   617	                Used &= ~REG_A;
   618	                Src->Flags |= LI_USED_BY_Y;
   619	                break;
   620	            case OP65_TXA:
   621	                Src = &LI->X;
   622	                Tgt = &LI->A;
   623	                Used &= ~REG_X;
   624	                Src->Flags |= LI_USED_BY_A;
   625	                break;
   626	            case OP65_TYA:
   627	                Src = &LI->Y;
   628	                Tgt = &LI->A;
   629	                Used &= ~REG_Y;
   630	                Src->Flags |= LI_USED_BY_A;
   631	                break;
   632	            case OP65_TSX:
   633	                ClearLoadRegInfo (&LI->X);
   634	                return Used;
   635	            case OP65_TXS:
   636	                return Used;
   637	            default:            Internal ("Unknown XFR insn in TrackLoads");
   638	        }
   639	
   640	        /* Transfer the data */
   641	        Tgt->LoadIndex  = Src->LoadIndex;
   642	        Tgt->LoadEntry  = Src->LoadEntry;
   643	        Tgt->LoadYIndex = Src->LoadYIndex;
   644	        Tgt->LoadYEntry = Src->LoadYEntry;
   645	        Tgt->ChgIndex   = I;
   646	        Tgt->Offs       = Src->Offs;
   647	        Tgt->Flags      = Src->Flags;
   648	
   649	    } else if (CE_IsCallTo (E, "ldaxysp") && RegValIsKnown (E->RI->In.RegY)) {
   650	
   651	        /* Both registers set, Y changed */
   652	        LI->A.LoadIndex = I;
   653	        LI->A.ChgIndex  = I;
   654	        LI->A.Flags     = (LI_LOAD_INSN | LI_DIRECT | LI_RELOAD_Y | LI_SP);
   655	        LI->A.Offs      = (unsigned char) E->RI->In.RegY - 1;
   656	
   657	        LI->X.LoadIndex = I;
   658	        LI->X.ChgIndex  = I;
   659	        LI->X.Flags     = (LI_LOAD_INSN | LI_DIRECT | LI_RELOAD_Y | LI_SP);
   660	        LI->X.Offs      = (unsigned char) E->RI->In.RegY;
   661	
   662	        /* Reg Y can be regarded as unused if this load is removed */
   663	        Used &= ~REG_Y;
   664	        LI->Y.Flags |= LI_USED_BY_A | LI_USED_BY_X;
   665	
   666	    } else {
   667	        HonourUseAndChg (&LI->A, REG_A, E, I);
   668	        HonourUseAndChg (&LI->X, REG_X, E, I);
   669	        HonourUseAndChg (&LI->Y, REG_Y, E, I);
   670	    }
   671	
   672	    return Used;
   673	}
   674	
   675	
   676	
   677	void SetDontRemoveEntryFlag (LoadRegInfo* LRI)
   678	/* Flag the entry as non-removable according to register flags */
   679	{
   680	    if (LRI->Flags & LI_DONT_REMOVE) {
   681	        if (LRI->LoadEntry != 0) {
   682	            LRI->LoadEntry->Flags |= CEF_DONT_REMOVE;
   683	
   684	            /* If the load requires Y, then Y shouldn't be removed either */
   685	            if (LRI->LoadYEntry != 0) {
   686	                LRI->LoadYEntry->Flags |= CEF_DONT_REMOVE;
   687	            }
   688	        }
   689	    }
   690	}
   691	
   692	
   693	
   694	void ResetDontRemoveEntryFlag (LoadRegInfo* LRI)
   695	/* Unflag the entry as non-removable according to register flags */
   696	{
   697	    if (LRI->LoadEntry != 0) {
   698	        LRI->LoadEntry->Flags &= ~CEF_DONT_REMOVE;
   699	    }
   700	
   701	    if (LRI->LoadYEntry != 0) {
   702	        LRI->LoadYEntry->Flags &= ~CEF_DONT_REMOVE;
   703	    }
   704	
   705	    if (LRI->ChgEntry != 0) {
   706	        LRI->ChgEntry->Flags &= ~CEF_DONT_REMOVE;
   707	    }
   708	}

   636	static void OptDebugOpt (const char* Opt attribute ((unused)), const char* Arg)
   637	/* Debug optimization steps */
   638	{
   639	    char Buf [128];
   640	    char* Line;
   641	
   642	    /* Open the file */
   643	    FILE* F = fopen (Arg, "r");
   644	    if (F == 0) {
   645	        AbEnd ("Cannot open '%s': %s", Arg, strerror (errno));
   646	    }
   647	
   648	    /* Read line by line, ignore empty lines and switch optimization
   649	    ** steps on/off.
   650	    */
   651	    while (fgets (Buf, sizeof (Buf), F) != 0) {
   652	
   653	        /* Remove trailing control chars. This will also remove the
   654	        ** trailing newline.
   655	        */
   656	        unsigned Len = strlen (Buf);
   657	        while (Len > 0 && IsControl (Buf[Len-1])) {
   658	            --Len;
   659	        }
   660	        Buf[Len] = '\0';
   661	
   662	        /* Get a pointer to the buffer and remove leading white space */
   663	        Line = Buf;
   664	        while (IsBlank (*Line)) {
   665	            ++Line;
   666	        }
   667	
   668	        /* Check the first character and enable/disable the step or
   669	        ** ignore the line
   670	        */
   671	        switch (*Line) {
   672	
   673	            case '\0':
   674	            case '#':
   675	            case ';':
   676	                /* Empty or comment line */
   677	                continue;
   678	
   679	            case '-':
   680	                DisableOpt (Line+1);
   681	                break;
   682	
   683	            case '+':
   684	                ++Line;
   685	                /* FALLTHROUGH */
   686	
   687	            default:
   688	                EnableOpt (Line);
   689	                break;
   690	
   691	        }
   692	
   693	    }
   694	
   695	    /* Close the file, no error check here since we were just reading and
   696	    ** this is only a debug function.
   697	    */
   698	    (void) fclose (F);
   699	}

OBSERVATION:
static unsigned Opt_a_tossub (StackOpData* D)
/* Optimize the tossubax sequence. */
{
    CodeEntry*  X;


    /* Inline the sbc */
    D->IP = D->OpIndex+1;

    if ((D->Rhs.X.Flags & LI_DIRECT) == 0) {
        /* The RHS high byte may be incomplete and carried over from the LHS in
        ** this RegA-only optimization, so RHS removal must not be relied on to
        ** leave the LHS value in A.
        */
        if ((D->Lhs.A.Flags & (LI_DIRECT | LI_RELOAD_Y)) == LI_DIRECT) {
            X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_LDA, D->Lhs.A.LoadEntry->AM, D->Lhs.A.LoadEntry->Arg, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
            InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
        } else {
            /* Save and reload LHS from temporary storage. Be sure to setup IP after
            ** adding the store, otherwise it may get shifted.
            */
            X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_STA, AM65_ZP, D->ZPLo, 0, D->PushEntry->LI);
            InsertEntry (D, X, D->PushIndex+1);
            D->IP = D->OpIndex+1;

            X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_LDA, AM65_ZP, D->ZPLo, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
            InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);
        }
    }

    /* Must be true because of OP_RHS_LOAD_DIRECT. Since this is a RegA-only
    ** optimization, only the low byte of RHS needs to be directly usable.
    */
    CHECK ((D->Rhs.A.Flags & LI_DIRECT) != 0);

    /* sec */
    X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_SEC, AM65_IMP, 0, 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
    InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);

    /* Add code for low operand */
    AddOpLow (D, OP65_SBC, &D->Rhs);

    /* Do sign-extension as high-byte operation only when its result is used */
    if ((GetRegInfo (D->Code, D->IP, REG_X) & REG_X) != 0) {
        CodeLabel* L;
        CodeEntry* N;

        X = NewCodeEntry (OP65_LDX, AM65_IMM, MakeHexArg (0), 0, D->OpEntry->LI);
        InsertEntry (D, X, D->IP++);

        /* Add sign extension - N is unused now */
        N = CS_GetEntry (D->Code, D->IP);
